\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l00513}00513 \textcolor{comment}{/* If you add a new statement below, make sure to add it to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l00515}00515 \textcolor{comment}{   sqlite3\_clear\_bindings()), using an un-\/prepared statement may}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01559}01559 \textcolor{comment}{    For performance, ideal to skip a member we've already added.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01933}01933 \textcolor{comment}{  TODO: I wonder if this can actually be cut (just here)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01934}01934 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01935}01935 \textcolor{comment}{  We were adding this "{}include"{} to the "{}includes"{} table alongside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01936}01936 \textcolor{comment}{  other includes (from a FileDef). However, FileDef and ClassDef are using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01937}01937 \textcolor{comment}{  "{}includes"{} nodes in very a different way:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01938}01938 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/ With FileDef, it means the file includes another.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01939}01939 \textcolor{comment}{  -\/ With ClassDef, it means you should include this file to use this class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01940}01940 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01941}01941 \textcolor{comment}{  Because of this difference, I added a column to compounddef, header\_id, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01942}01942 \textcolor{comment}{  linked it back to the appropriate file. We could just add a nullable text}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01943}01943 \textcolor{comment}{  column that would hold a string equivalent to what the HTML docs include,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01944}01944 \textcolor{comment}{  but the logic for generating it is embedded in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01945}01945 \textcolor{comment}{  ClassDef::writeIncludeFiles(OutputList \&ol).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01946}01946 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01947}01947 \textcolor{comment}{  That said, at least on the handful of test sets I have, header\_id == file\_id,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01948}01948 \textcolor{comment}{  suggesting it could be cut and clients might be able to reconstruct it from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01949}01949 \textcolor{comment}{  other values if there's a solid heuristic for *when a class will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01950}01950 \textcolor{comment}{  have a header file*.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2src_2sqlite3gen_8cpp_source_l01951}01951 \textcolor{comment}{  */}}
